# .10 SILYL CATIONS.1I SILYL[°A TLNN

Given that silicon is more electropositive than carbon, it may be surprising that silyl anionsiventhtsilconismoeelectopostve thncabon,itmaybe surorising tht silvlanion are much more stable than the analogous carbanions, whereas silyl cations are less stablere much more sablethn the anlogouscabnions,whereassilylcaionsarelessable than the analogous carbocations. Multiple factors account for these differences. As men-hn the analogous crboeatons.Nutple tacos account tor these derences.As men tioned, the stability of silyl anions reflects the relative stability of the 3s electron pair,oned the stablrv ot slv anons reecs the reve sablv ot the 3s elecron nar relative to the 3p electrons; the 3s–3p energy gap is significantly higher than thetve to the3pelctons;the 3s-penegy gpis sgnncantyhgher than t $2 \mathrm { s } { - } 2 \mathrm { p }$ gap.
